<script type="text/javascript">
function contentTSR(){
	var totalHeadline = 10;
	
	if(content_tsr_automate == true){
		var tsr_curContent = totalHeadline;
	} else {
		var tsr_curContent = 0;
	}
	var tsr_aTx;

	// configure block
	$("#contentTSR").css("background-color", content_tsr_mainbg);
	$("#contentTSR-title").css({"border-bottom": "1px solid "+content_tsr_title_stroke});
	$("#contentTSR-title .titleText").css("color", content_tsr_title_text);
	$(".contentTSR-main-bg").css("background-color", content_tsr_middlebg);
	$(".contentTSR-headline a").css("color", content_tsr_headline_text);
	$(".contentTSR-summary").css("color", content_tsr_summary_text);
	$(".contentTSR-more a").css("color", content_tsr_more_text);
	$("#contentTSR-thumbwrapper").css({"border-top": "1px solid "+content_tsr_thumb_stroke});
	$(".contentTSR-thumb-off").css("border", "1px solid "+content_tsr_thumb_off);
	$("#contentTSR-popup img").css("border", "3px solid "+content_tsr_popup);
	$("#contentTSR-title span").html(content_tsr_title);
	
	
	function initTSRContent(){
		tsr_parseXML(this);
		tsr_setInteraction();
	}
	
	var iNum = 0;
	
	function tsr_parseXML(xml){
//alert("contentTSR-main-bg width: " + $(".contentTSR-main-bg").width());
		if($("#contentTSR").width() >= 645){
			$("#contentTSR").width(645);
			$(".contentTSR-headline").addClass("contentTSR-headline-645").removeClass("contentTSR-headline");
			$(".contentTSR-summary").addClass("contentTSR-summary-645").removeClass("contentTSR-summary");
			var headClass = "contentTSR-headline-645";
			var sumClass = "contentTSR-summary-645";
			$("#contentTSR-controls").css("left", ($("#contentTSR").width()-90)+"px").show();
			totalHeadline = 10;
		}else{
			$("#contentTSR").css("width", "505px");
			$(".contentTSR-headline").addClass("contentTSR-headline-505").removeClass("contentTSR-headline");
			$(".contentTSR-summary").addClass("contentTSR-summary-505").removeClass("contentTSR-summary");
			var headClass = "contentTSR-headline-505";
			var sumClass = "contentTSR-summary-505";
			$("#contentTSR-controls").show();
			totalHeadline = 7;
		}
		$(".contentTSR-main-bg").css({"width": (parseInt($("#contentTSR").css("width")) - parseInt($(".contentTSR-image").css("width"))) + "px", "overflow": "hidden"}).show();
		$(".contentTSR-main").css({"width": (parseInt($("#contentTSR").css("width")) - parseInt($(".contentTSR-image").css("width"))) + "px", "overflow": "hidden"});
//alert("contentTSR-main-bg width (css): " + $(".contentTSR-main-bg").css("width"));
		
	
		if(xml == "local"){
			var fullFeed = $("features");
		}else{
			var fullFeed = xml.response.responseXML;
			fullFeed = fullFeed.firstChild;
		}
		function buildTSR(item){
			// BUILD HREF
			var iType = $(item).find("type:first").text();
			var iHREF = "";
			if(xml == "local"){
				if(iType == "S"){
                iHREF = "http:/"+"/"+document.domain+"/story/" + $(item).find("id:first").text() + "/story";
}else if(iType == "C"){
                iHREF = "http:/"+"/"+document.domain+"/category/" + $(item).find("id:first").text() + "/category";

				}
			}else{
if(iType == "S"){
                iHREF = "http:/"+"/"+document.domain+"/story/" + $(item).find("id:first").text() + "/story";
}else if(iType == "C"){
                iHREF = "http:/"+"/"+document.domain+"/category/" + $(item).find("id:first").text() + "/category";

				}
			}		
			// SET REUSEABLE ATTRIBS
			var iHeadline = $(item).find("headline:first").text();
			var iTitle = iHeadline.replace("'","`");
			var iImg = $(item).find("filename:first").text();
			if(iImg == ""){
				iImg = content_tsr_backupImg;
			}
//

			// WRITE BUTTONS
			$("#contentTSR-thumbwrapper img[rel='" + iNum + "']").attr("src", iImg).show();
			
			// WRITE MAIN PANELS
			$(".contentTSR-image[rel='"+iNum+"'] a").attr({"title": iTitle, "href": iHREF}).find("img").attr("src", iImg);
			//$(".contentTSR-main[rel='"+iNum+"'] ." + headClass + " a").attr("title", iTitle)
			//$(".contentTSR-main[rel='"+iNum+"'] ." + headClass + " a").attr("href", iHREF)
			$(".contentTSR-main[rel='"+iNum+"'] ." + headClass + " a").html(ellipses(iHeadline, headClass));
			//$(".contentTSR-main[rel='"+iNum+"'] ." + headClass).html("<a href='"+iHREF+"' style='font:bold 14px Arial,Verdana,sans-serif; color:#3f7f00;' title='"+iTitle+"'>"+ellipses(iHeadline, headClass)+"</a>");
			$(".contentTSR-main[rel='"+iNum+"'] .contentTSR-more a").attr("title", iTitle).attr("href", iHREF);
			$(".contentTSR-main[rel='"+iNum+"'] ." + sumClass).html(ellipses($(item).find("abstract:first").text(), sumClass));

//$("#debug").text($("#debug").text() + ", " + iNum + ": " + $(".contentTSR-main[rel='"+iNum+"'] ." + headClass).html());

			// >>> next
			iNum++;
			//$("#debug").text(iNum);
		}
		for(var ii=0;ii<20;ii++){
			$(fullFeed).children("[displaysize='-20'][displayorder='"+(ii+1)+"']").each(function(){
				if(iNum >=totalHeadline){
					return;
				}
				buildTSR(this);
			});
			$(fullFeed).children("[displaysize='-10'][displayorder='"+(ii+1)+"']").each(function(){
				if(iNum >=totalHeadline){
					return;
				}
				buildTSR(this);
			});
			$(fullFeed).children("[displaysize='-7'][displayorder='"+(ii+1)+"']").each(function(){
				if(iNum >=totalHeadline){
					return;
				}
				buildTSR(this);
			});
			$(fullFeed).children("[displaysize='-1'][displayorder='"+(ii+1)+"']").each(function(){
				if(iNum >=totalHeadline){
					return;
				}
				buildTSR(this);
			});
//$("#debug").text($("#debug").text() + ", " + ii + ": " + $(".contentTSR-image[rel='"+1+"'] a").attr("title"));
		}
		if(iNum < $("#contentTSR-thumbwrapper img[class='contentTSR-thumb-off']").length){
			for(xx=iNum; xx<$("#contentTSR-thumbwrapper img[class='contentTSR-thumb-off']").length; xx++){
				$("#contentTSR-thumbwrapper img[rel='" + xx + "']").hide();
			}
			//totalHeadline = iNum;
		}
	
		$(".contentTSR-main:first").show().attr("name", "active");
		$(".contentTSR-image:first").show().attr("name", "active");
		$("#contentTSR-thumbwrapper").show();
	}
	
	function tsr_setInteraction(){
		$("#contentTSR-thumbwrapper img[class='contentTSR-thumb-off']").click(function(){
			var cur_id = $(this).attr("rel");
			clearTimeout(tsr_aTx);
			content_tsr_automate = false;
			if (tsr_curContent != cur_id) {
				tsr_curContent = cur_id;
				tsr_show_content();
			}
		})
	
		$("#contentTSR-thumbwrapper").mousemove(function(e){
			$("#contentTSR-popup").css("left", e.pageX-58-$(this).offset().left);
		});	
	
		$("#contentTSR-thumbwrapper img[class='contentTSR-thumb-off']").hover(
			function(){
				$("#contentTSR-popup img").attr("src", $(this).attr("src")).parent().show();
			},
			function(){
				$("#contentTSR-popup").hide();
			}
		);

// WORKAROUND vvvv
		$(".contentTSR-main").each(function(){
			$(this).find("a").mouseover(function(){
				$(this).attr({"href": $(".contentTSR-image[rel='" + tsr_curContent + "'] a").attr("href"), "title": $(".contentTSR-image[rel='" + tsr_curContent + "'] a").attr("title")});
				//alert($(this).attr("href"));
			});
		})
// WORKAROUND ^^^^
	
		$("#contentTSR-controls img").each(function(){
			$(this).click(function(){
				if($(this).attr("rel") == "f"){
					clearTimeout(tsr_aTx);
					content_tsr_automate = false;
					tsr_curContent++;
					$("#contentTSR-controls img[rel='ps']").attr({"rel": "pl", "src": "http://ftpcontent.worldnow.com/revenue/tsr/food/food-content_tsr_play.png"});
					tsr_show_content();
				}
				else if($(this).attr("rel") == "b"){
					clearTimeout(tsr_aTx);
					content_tsr_automate = false;
					tsr_curContent--;
					$("#contentTSR-controls img[rel='ps']").attr({"rel": "pl", "src": "http://ftpcontent.worldnow.com/revenue/tsr/food/food-content_tsr_play.png"});
					tsr_show_content();
				}
				else if($(this).attr("rel") == "ps"){
					clearTimeout(tsr_aTx);
					content_tsr_automate = false;
					$(this).attr({"rel": "pl", "src": "http://ftpcontent.worldnow.com/revenue/tsr/food/food-content_tsr_play.png"});
				}
				else if($(this).attr("rel") == "pl"){
					content_tsr_automate = true;
					tsr_show_content();
					$(this).attr({"rel": "ps", "src": "http://ftpcontent.worldnow.com/revenue/tsr/food/food-content_tsr_pause.png"});
				}
			});
		});
	}
	
	function tsr_show_content(){
		clearTimeout(tsr_aTx);
		if(content_tsr_automate == true){
			tsr_curContent++;
			tsr_aTx = setTimeout(tsr_show_content, content_tsr_timer*1000);
			$("#contentTSR-controls img[rel='pl']").attr({"rel": "ps", "src": "http://ftpcontent.worldnow.com/revenue/tsr/food/food-content_tsr_pause.png"});
		}else{
			$("#contentTSR-controls img[rel='ps']").attr({"rel": "pl", "src": "http://ftpcontent.worldnow.com/revenue/tsr/food/food-content_tsr_play.png"});
		}
		if(tsr_curContent >= totalHeadline){
			tsr_curContent = 0
		};
		if(tsr_curContent < 0){
			tsr_curContent = totalHeadline - 1;
		};
		
		$(".contentTSR-image[rel!='"+tsr_curContent+"'][name='active']").each(function(){
			$(this).fadeOut(600).attr("name", "");
		});
		$(".contentTSR-main[rel!='"+tsr_curContent+"'][name='active']").each(function(){
			$(this).fadeOut(600).attr("name", "");
		})
		
		$(".contentTSR-image[rel='"+tsr_curContent+"']").fadeIn(500).attr("name", "active");
		$(".contentTSR-main[rel='"+tsr_curContent+"']").fadeIn(500).attr("name", "active");
		$(".contentTSR-thumb-on").each(function(){
			$(this).removeClass("contentTSR-thumb-on").css({"left": (parseInt($(this).css("left"))+1)+"px", "top": "10px", "border": "1px solid "+content_tsr_thumb_off});
		});
		$(".contentTSR-thumb-off[rel='"+tsr_curContent+"']").each(function(){
			$(this).addClass("contentTSR-thumb-on").css({"left": (parseInt($(this).css("left"))-1)+"px", "top": "9px", "border": "2px solid "+content_tsr_thumb_on});
		});
		
	}
	
	function tsr_errorFunction(e){
		//$(".tsr_title_text").html("Error Loading");
	}
	
	if(document.location.toString().indexOf("http://")!=-1){
		WNHttpRequestManager.makeRequest("http://api.worldnow.com/feed/v2.0/categories/" + content_tsr_feedNo + "/all?alt=xml", { onSuccess: initTSRContent, onError: tsr_errorFunction});
	}else{
		tsr_parseXML('local');
		tsr_setInteraction();
	}
	//tsr_setInteraction();
	$(document).ready(function(){
		setTimeout(tsr_show_content, 1000);
	});
}
contentTSR();
</script></div></div><!--END wnDSItems-->
</div><!--
				END wnDS29-->
